    <script>
      const originalConsoleError = console.error;
      console.error = function(...args) {
        originalConsoleError.apply(console, args);
        
        // Filter out React devtools warnings if any
        if (args[0] && typeof args[0] === 'string' && args[0].includes('Warning:')) return;
        
        let msg = args.map(a => (typeof a === 'object' && a !== null) ? (a.stack || a.message || JSON.stringify(a)) : a).join(' ');
        
        if (!document.getElementById('console-error-display')) {
          const div = document.createElement('div');
          div.id = 'console-error-display';
          div.style = 'position:fixed; bottom:0; left:0; right:0; z-index:999999; background:rgba(220,38,38,0.9); color:white; padding:10px; max-height: 50vh; overflow-y:auto; font-family:monospace; font-size:12px;';
          document.body.appendChild(div);
        }
        
        const el = document.getElementById('console-error-display');
        el.innerHTML += `<div style="border-bottom:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.2); padding:5px 0;">$[CONSOLE ERROR] ${msg}</div>`;
      };

      window.onerror = function(message, source, lineno, colno, error) {
        console.error("Intercepted by onerror:", message, error);
        document.body.innerHTML += `
          <div style="background-color: #0f172a; color: #f8fafc; min-height: 100vh; display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center; font-family: sans-serif; padding: 20px; z-index:9999; position:fixed; inset:0;">
            <div style="background-color: #1e293b; border-top: 5px solid #ef4444; border-radius: 8px; padding: 30px; max-width: 800px; width: 100%; box-shadow: 0 25px 50px -12px rgba(0,0,0,0.5);">
              <h1 style="font-size: 1.5rem; color: #fca5a5; margin-bottom: 15px;">Fatal UI Error</h1>
              <div style="background-color: #0f172a; padding: 15px; border-left: 4px solid #ef4444; margin-bottom: 20px;">
                <p style="margin: 0 0 10px 0;"><strong>Error Message:</strong> <span style="color: #fca5a5;">${message}</span></p>
                <p style="margin: 0;"><strong>Location:</strong> Line <span style="color: #60a5fa;">${lineno}</span> in ${source}</p>
              </div>
              <div style="background-color: #020617; color: #10b981; padding: 15px; overflow-x: auto; font-family: monospace; font-size: 0.85rem;">
                ${error && error.stack ? error.stack.replace(/\n/g, '<br>') : 'Stack trace unavailable. Please check the browser console.'}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        `;
        return true; 
      };
    </script>
